CooldekĠcladdingĠprovidesĠaĠroofĠinsulationĠandĠceiling-likeĠfinishĠin-one.ĠOptionsĠAvailableĠChooseĠfromĠeitherĠtheĠCooldekĠClassicĠorĠtheĠCooldekĠCGIĠroofĠprofiles.ĠThereĠareĠthreeĠinsulationĠthicknessesĠtoĠchooseĠfrom;Ġ50mm,Ġ75mmĠandĠ100mm.ĠAllĠpanelsĠhaveĠaĠwidthĠcoverageÂłofĠ1000mm.ĠChooseĠtheĠcorrectĠlengthĠforĠyourĠprojectĠsizeĠfromĠtheĠdropdown.ĠTheĠtopsideĠcolourĠchoicesĠincludeĠaĠwideĠrangeĠofĠpopularĠcoloursĠtoĠhelpĠintegrateĠyourĠCooldekĠRoofingĠintoĠexistingĠcolourĠschemes.ĠTheĠundersideĠisĠavailableĠinĠOffĠWhite.ĠOutbackÂ®ÂłPatioĠWithĠInsulatedĠCooldekÂ®ĠControlĠtheĠclimate,ĠkeepĠcoolĠandĠexperienceĠoutdoorĠlivingĠinĠcomfortĠunderĠaĠStratcoĠOutbackÂ®ĠwithĠCooldekÂ®Ġroofing.ĠWhenĠincorporatedĠwithĠaĠStratcoĠOutbackĠPatioĠtheĠinnovativeĠCooldekĠinsulatedĠpanelĠprovidesĠaĠroof,ĠinsulationĠandĠceilingĠlikeĠfinishĠallĠinĠoneĠproduct,ĠwithĠsuperiorĠspanningĠcapabilitiesĠandĠoutstandingĠcoolingĠperformance.ĠAddĠvalueĠandĠextendĠyourĠoutdoorĠlivingĠallĠyearĠroundĠwithĠaĠStratcoĠOutbackĠandĠCooldekĠRoofing.ĠStrengthĠAndĠVersatilityĠ ExceptionalĠstrengthĠallowsĠCooldekĠtoĠspanĠupĠtoĠanĠimpressiveĠsevenĠmetres.ĠLargeĠspansĠreduceĠtheĠnumberĠofĠsupportingĠbeamsĠandĠframework,ĠwhichĠcreatesĠanĠunclutteredĠceiling-likeĠappearance.ĠSimpleĠtoĠinstall,ĠCooldekĠevenĠhasĠanĠinbuiltĠrebateĠwithinĠitĠtoĠconcealĠelectricalĠwiringĠforĠfansĠandĠlightĠfittings.ĠStratcoĠCooldekĠhasĠbeenĠdesigned,ĠengineeredĠandĠtestedĠtoĠcomplyĠwithĠallĠrelevantĠAustralianĠStandards.ĠInvestĠInĠCooldekĠRoofingĠĠClassicĠsteelĠroofĠlookĠonĠtop,ĠwithĠaĠsmoothĠceiling-likeĠunderside.ĠOutstandingĠcoolingĠperformance.ĠChooseĠfromĠCooldekĠClassicĠorĠCooldekĠCGIĠroofĠprofiles.ĠChooseĠfromĠthreeĠinsulationĠthicknesses.ĠWideĠrangeĠofĠpopularĠroofĠcolours.ĠCeiling-likeĠundersideĠisĠavailableĠinĠWhiteĠorĠaĠchoiceĠofĠhighĠglossĠcolours.ĠExceptionalĠstrengthĠreducesĠtheĠnumberĠofĠbeamsĠandĠframeworkĠrequired.ĠReducesĠheatĠtoĠmakeĠyourĠoutdoorĠlivingĠareaĠmoreĠcomfortable.ĠSavesĠonĠelectricityĠbyĠreducingĠindoorĠcoolingĠcosts.ĠĠSpecificationsĠCooldekĠpanelsĠhaveĠtheĠfollowingĠinsulationĠratingĠ(RĠvalue):ĠĠ50mmĠthickĠpanelsĠâĢĵĠupĠtoĠR1.48Ġ75mmĠthickĠpanelsĠâĢĵĠupĠtoĠR2.11Ġ100mmĠthickĠpanelsĠâĢĵĠupĠtoĠR2.75

antonĠ RacingĠProductsĠhasĠbeenĠbuildingĠoilĠpansĠandĠengineĠrelatedĠproductsĠforĠracingĠandĠhighĠperformanceĠapplicationsĠsinceĠ1981.ĠWeĠbeganĠinĠaĠsmallĠConnecticutĠgarageĠbuildingĠspecialtyĠoilĠpansĠforĠlocalĠautoĠracers.ĠTheĠuniqueĠoilĠpansĠprovidedĠracersĠwithĠtheĠpowerĠandĠqualityĠtheyĠdemanded.ĠAsĠpopularityĠforĠtheĠspecialtyĠoilĠpansĠgrewĠsoĠdidĠourĠselectionĠofĠproducts.ĠTodayĠweĠofferĠaĠwideĠrangeĠofĠhighĠperformanceĠproductsĠforĠracingĠandĠtheĠstreet.ĠDuringĠourĠbusinessĠhoursĠeveryĠphoneĠcallĠisĠdirectedĠstraightĠtoĠourĠhardĠworkingĠsalesĠteam.ĠTheyĠareĠhappyĠtoĠuseĠtheirĠexperienceĠandĠknowledgeĠinĠtheĠautomotiveĠmarketĠtoĠprovideĠcustomerĠservice,ĠproductĠadvice,ĠandĠtechnicalĠsupportĠtoĠyouĠandĠyourĠcustomer.ĠOurĠproductionĠprocessĠfocusesĠonĠaccuracyĠandĠreliability.ĠEveryĠproductĠweĠmakeĠisĠbuiltĠwithĠtheĠsameĠproductionĠandĠqualityĠassuranceĠmethodsĠthatĠweĠuseĠwhenĠbuildingĠpartsĠforĠFord,ĠRoush,ĠandĠMopar.ĠAllĠproductsĠareĠtigĠwelded,ĠratherĠthenĠmigĠwelded.ĠTheĠtigĠweldingĠprocessĠtakesĠmoreĠtimeĠandĠskillĠbutĠensuresĠmoreĠevenĠheatĠandĠpenetrationĠthroughĠoutĠtheĠweldingĠprocess.ĠThisĠresultĠisĠbetterĠqualityĠweldsĠwithĠlessĠpossibilityĠforĠleaksĠandĠcracks.ĠEveryĠoilĠpan,ĠvalveĠcover,ĠandĠtankĠthatĠweĠproduceĠunderĠgoesĠseveralĠleakĠtests.ĠOurĠoilĠpansĠandĠvalveĠcoversĠareĠfittedĠonĠblocksĠorĠheadsĠseveralĠtimesĠthroughĠoutĠtheĠproductionĠprocessĠtoĠensureĠtheyĠeasilyĠinstallĠonĠtheirĠapplication.ĠWeĠhaveĠbeenĠactivelyĠinvolvedĠinĠracingĠforĠdecades.ĠOverĠtheĠyearsĠweĠhaveĠbuiltĠandĠranĠseveralĠcarsĠandĠhaveĠanĠappreciationĠforĠtheĠeffortĠandĠdedicationĠitĠtakesĠcompete.ĠWeĠactivelyĠparticipateĠwithĠclubs,Ġschools,ĠandĠotherĠorganizationsĠinĠtheĠperformanceĠautomotiveĠcommunity.

HowĠdoesĠitĠwork?ĠTheĠiDRIVEĠthrottleĠcontrollerĠmodifiesĠtheĠvoltageĠsignalĠfromĠtheĠflyĠbyĠwireĠpedalĠassemblyĠtoĠallowĠyouĠtoĠtuneĠtheĠresponseĠfromĠyourĠacceleratorĠpedalĠandĠgreatlyĠreduceĠtheĠdeadĠzoneĠfromĠwhenĠyouĠinitiallyĠdepressĠtheĠpedalĠcommonlyĠreferredĠtoĠasĠthrottleĠlag.ĠTheĠiDRIVEĠdoesĠnotĠplugĠintoĠtheĠOBDIIĠport.DoesĠiDRIVEĠincreaseĠpowerĠoutput?ĠNo,ĠiDRIVEĠthrottleĠcontrollersĠwontĠincreaseĠpowerĠoutput.ĠTheyĠhaveĠnoĠcontrolĠoverĠfuelĠmapping,ĠairĠfuelĠratioĠorĠinjectionĠtimingĠetc.ĠiDRIVEsĠsimplyĠchangeĠtheĠwayĠyourĠthrottleĠrespondsĠforĠsharperĠresponse.ĠAlthoughĠtheĠexactĠresultĠisĠhardĠtoĠexplainĠitĠbasicallyĠwakesĠtheĠcarĠupĠandĠmakesĠtheĠaccelerationĠfeelĠlessĠlazy.IsĠiDRIVEĠsuitableĠforĠTowing?ĠiDRIVEĠthrottleĠcontrollersĠareĠveryĠusefulĠforĠtowingĠasĠtheyĠhelpĠtoĠgetĠtheĠvehicleĠmovingĠwithĠlessĠeffort,ĠespeciallyĠusefulĠforĠtowingĠaroundĠtownĠwhereĠthereĠisĠaĠlotĠofĠstoppingĠandĠstarting.IsĠiDRIVEĠsuitableĠforĠManualĠTransmission?ĠiDRIVEĠthrottleĠcontrollersĠareĠsuitedĠtoĠbothĠAutomaticĠandĠManualĠtransmission.IsĠiDRIVEĠhardĠtoĠinstall?ĠOnĠmostĠvehiclesĠanĠiDRIVEĠcanĠbeĠinstalledĠinĠlessĠthanĠ2ĠminutesĠwithĠnoĠspecialĠtoolsĠorĠtechnicalĠknowledgeĠrequired.ĠItĠisĠaĠsimpleĠplugĠandĠplayĠdeviceĠthatĠisĠdesignedĠtoĠspecificallyĠintegrateĠintoĠyourĠvehicle.IsĠiDRIVEĠuniversalĠorĠvehicleĠspecific?ĠAlthoughĠthereĠareĠmanyĠsharedĠapplications,ĠeachĠiDRIVEĠapplicationĠisĠrelativelyĠuniqueĠtoĠeachĠvehicle.ĠPleaseĠcheckĠourĠapplicationĠguideĠtoĠseeĠifĠyourĠmodelĠisĠavailable.ĠIfĠyouĠdonâĢĻtĠseeĠyourĠvehicleĠlistedĠpleaseĠfeelĠfreeĠtoĠcontactĠusĠtoĠcheckĠasĠweĠareĠaddingĠnewĠapplicationsĠallĠtheĠtime.IsĠiDRIVEĠsuitableĠforĠpetrolĠvehicles?ĠTheĠiDRIVEĠthrottleĠcontrollerĠcanĠbeĠusedĠonĠbothĠnaturallyĠaspiratedĠandĠforcedĠinductionĠPetrolĠandĠDieselĠengines.CanâĢĻtĠIĠjustĠpressĠtheĠacceleratorĠdownĠfasterĠtoĠreplicateĠtheĠsameĠresponse?ĠIDRIVEĠthrottleĠcontrollersĠworkĠinĠ2Ġways.ĠWhenĠyouĠfirstĠdepressĠtheĠpedalĠthereĠisĠwhatĠisĠreferredĠtoĠasĠaĠdeadĠzoneĠwhereĠthereĠisĠveryĠlittleĠresponse,ĠnoĠmatterĠhowĠhardĠorĠfastĠyouĠhitĠtheĠpedalĠyouĠcanâĢĻtĠovercomeĠthis.ĠTheĠiDRIVEĠconvertsĠthisĠsignalĠtoĠaction,ĠgreatlyĠreducingĠthisĠdeadĠzone.ĠTheĠsecondĠpartĠisĠopeningĠtheĠthrottleĠearlierĠinĠtheĠpedalĠstroke,ĠinĠtheoryĠyouĠmightĠbeĠableĠtoĠreplicateĠthisĠbyĠpressingĠtheĠpedalĠfasterĠandĠharder,ĠbutĠinĠpracticeĠyouĠcanâĢĻt.ĠForĠanyoneĠwhoĠdoubtsĠtheĠeffectivenessĠofĠanĠiDRIVEĠthrottleĠcontroller,ĠIĠhighlyĠrecommendĠtakingĠadvantageĠofĠourĠ30ĠdayĠmoneyĠbackĠguarantee.ĠIfĠyouĠareĠnotĠ100%ĠhappyĠwithĠtheĠresultĠyouĠcanĠsendĠitĠbackĠforĠaĠfullĠrefundĠâĢĵĠnoĠquestionsĠasked.ĠWhenĠtheĠiDRIVEĠwasĠfirstĠlaunchedĠonĠtheĠmarket,ĠonĠoneĠofĠtheĠFordĠRangersĠforumsĠthereĠwasĠaĠgentĠwhoĠconstantlyĠtoldĠperspectiveĠcustomersĠtheyĠwereĠwastingĠtheirĠmoneyĠandĠcouldĠjustĠputĠtheirĠfootĠdownĠharderĠtoĠgetĠtheĠsameĠresult.ĠAfterĠweeksĠofĠthisĠpersonsĠnegativeĠcommentsĠâĢĵĠIĠofferedĠtoĠsendĠhimĠoneĠwithĠanĠinvoice.ĠIfĠheĠwasĠhappyĠwithĠitĠheĠcouldĠpayĠtheĠinvoice,ĠifĠnotĠIĠwouldĠpayĠforĠtheĠreturnĠpostage.ĠNotĠonlyĠdidĠheĠpayĠtheĠinvoice,ĠheĠthenĠwentĠonĠtoĠpostĠaĠfullĠapologyĠandĠveryĠgenerousĠproductĠreview.WillĠiDRIVEĠworkĠwithĠotherĠmodifications?ĠAftermarketĠCruiseĠControlĠâĢĵĠYes,ĠtoĠdateĠweĠhaveĠnotĠseenĠanĠaftermarketĠcruiseĠcontrolĠthatĠwonâĢĻtĠworkĠwithĠanĠiDRIVEĠincludingĠunitsĠthatĠplugĠdirectlyĠintoĠtheĠflyĠbyĠwireĠsystem.ĠECUĠTuneĠ/Ġ ReflashĠâĢĵĠYes,ĠiDRIVEĠthrottleĠcontrollersĠcanĠstillĠbeĠusedĠafterĠanĠECUĠtune/reflash.ĠInĠmostĠinstancesĠtunersĠdonâĢĻtĠchangeĠthrottleĠparameters.ĠEvenĠwhenĠthrottleĠparametersĠareĠchangedĠtheĠadjustabilityĠofĠthrottleĠresponseĠthatĠtheĠiDRIVEĠprovidesĠcanĠstillĠbeĠquiteĠuseful.ĠPowerĠChipsĠ/ĠExhaustĠâĢĵĠYes,ĠPowerĠchipsĠandĠupgradedĠexhaustĠsystemĠworkĠonĠaĠdifferentĠpartĠofĠtheĠcarĠsoĠanĠiDRIVEĠwillĠonlyĠcomplimentĠtheĠpositiveĠeffectsĠofĠchipsĠandĠexhausts.WillĠanĠiDRIVEĠvoidĠmyĠnewĠcarĠwarranty?ĠAnyĠaftermarket/nongenuineĠmodificationĠyouĠmakeĠtoĠyourĠnewĠcarĠwillĠhaveĠsomeĠimpactĠonĠyourĠnewĠcarĠwarranty,ĠifĠitĠisĠdeemedĠtoĠhaveĠcausedĠtheĠissueĠyouĠareĠseekingĠwarrantyĠon.ĠInĠrespectĠtoĠiDRIVE,ĠiDRIVEĠAustraliaĠhasĠdoneĠextensiveĠtestingĠtoĠensureĠaĠcorrectlyĠfittedĠiDRIVEĠwontĠdamageĠyourĠvehicle.ĠTheĠiDRIVEĠhasĠbeenĠdesignedĠsoĠthatĠifĠitĠdevelopsĠaĠfault,ĠtheĠvehicleĠcanĠbeĠputĠbackĠtoĠfactoryĠsettingsĠandĠtheĠvehicleĠwillĠreturnĠtoĠnormalĠoperation.ĠSoĠifĠyouĠareĠeverĠconcerned,ĠsimplyĠremoveĠtheĠiDRIVEĠandĠplugĠtheĠfactoryĠwiringĠbackĠintoĠtheĠpedalĠassembly.ĠInĠtheĠunlikelyĠeventĠthatĠtheĠiDRIVEĠdoesĠdamageĠyourĠvehicleĠtheĠiDRIVEĠisĠfullyĠcoveredĠbyĠourĠproductĠliabilityĠinsurance.MyĠiDRIVEĠdoesnâĢĻtĠturnĠoff?ĠiDRIVEĠthrottleĠcontrollersĠdonâĢĻtĠrequireĠthereĠownĠpowerĠsource.ĠTheyĠrelyĠonĠpowerĠfromĠtheĠacceleratorĠpedal.ĠInĠmanyĠvehicles,ĠwhenĠpowerĠtoĠtheĠignitionĠisĠcutĠmanyĠaccessoriesĠtakeĠsomeĠtimeĠtoĠpowerĠdown.ĠYouĠmayĠfindĠitĠwillĠtakeĠ30ĠsecondsĠbeforeĠyourĠiDRIVEĠturnsĠoff.ĠItĠmayĠalsoĠturnĠoffĠduringĠperiodsĠofĠinactivityĠsuchĠasĠwhenĠcruiseĠcontrolĠisĠinĠoperation.ĠSimplyĠtouchingĠtheĠacceleratorĠwillĠinstantlyĠturnĠitĠon.iDriveĠAustraliaĠhasĠrecentlyĠrebrandedĠtoĠbeĠcalledĠâĢĺUltimateĠ9âĢĻ,ĠandĠallĠnewĠmodelsĠofĠiDriveĠthrottleĠcontrollersĠareĠchangingĠtoĠshowĠâĢĺUltimateĠPerformanceâĢĻĠonĠtheĠproduct.ĠYouĠcanĠbeĠassuredĠthatĠtheseĠareĠ100%ĠauthenticĠiDriveĠthrottleĠcontrollers!

CantonĠ RacingĠProductsĠhasĠbeenĠbuildingĠoilĠpansĠandĠengineĠrelatedĠproductsĠforĠracingĠandĠhighĠperformanceĠapplicationsĠsinceĠ1981.ĠWeĠbeganĠinĠaĠsmallĠConnecticutĠgarageĠbuildingĠspecialtyĠoilĠpansĠforĠlocalĠautoĠracers.ĠTheĠuniqueĠoilĠpansĠprovidedĠracersĠwithĠtheĠpowerĠandĠqualityĠtheyĠdemanded.ĠAsĠpopularityĠforĠtheĠspecialtyĠoilĠpansĠgrewĠsoĠdidĠourĠselectionĠofĠproducts.ĠTodayĠweĠofferĠaĠwideĠrangeĠofĠhighĠperformanceĠproductsĠforĠracingĠandĠtheĠstreet.ĠDuringĠourĠbusinessĠhoursĠeveryĠphoneĠcallĠisĠdirectedĠstraightĠtoĠourĠhardĠworkingĠsalesĠteam.ĠTheyĠareĠhappyĠtoĠuseĠtheirĠexperienceĠandĠknowledgeĠinĠtheĠautomotiveĠmarketĠtoĠprovideĠcustomerĠservice,ĠproductĠadvice,ĠandĠtechnicalĠsupportĠtoĠyouĠandĠyourĠcustomer.ĠOurĠproductionĠprocessĠfocusesĠonĠaccuracyĠandĠreliability.ĠEveryĠproductĠweĠmakeĠisĠbuiltĠwithĠtheĠsameĠproductionĠandĠqualityĠassuranceĠmethodsĠthatĠweĠuseĠwhenĠbuildingĠpartsĠforĠFord,ĠRoush,ĠandĠMopar.ĠAllĠproductsĠareĠtigĠwelded,ĠratherĠthenĠmigĠwelded.ĠTheĠtigĠweldingĠprocessĠtakesĠmoreĠtimeĠandĠskillĠbutĠensuresĠmoreĠevenĠheatĠandĠpenetrationĠthroughĠoutĠtheĠweldingĠprocess.ĠThisĠresultĠisĠbetterĠqualityĠweldsĠwithĠlessĠpossibilityĠforĠleaksĠandĠcracks.ĠEveryĠoilĠpan,ĠvalveĠcover,ĠandĠtankĠthatĠweĠproduceĠunderĠgoesĠseveralĠleakĠtests.ĠOurĠoilĠpansĠandĠvalveĠcoversĠareĠfittedĠonĠblocksĠorĠheadsĠseveralĠtimesĠthroughĠoutĠtheĠproductionĠprocessĠtoĠensureĠtheyĠeasilyĠinstallĠonĠtheirĠapplication.ĠWeĠhaveĠbeenĠactivelyĠinvolvedĠinĠracingĠforĠdecades.ĠOverĠtheĠyearsĠweĠhaveĠbuiltĠandĠranĠseveralĠcarsĠandĠhaveĠanĠappreciationĠforĠtheĠeffortĠandĠdedicationĠitĠtakesĠcompete.ĠWeĠactivelyĠparticipateĠwithĠclubs,Ġschools,ĠandĠotherĠorganizationsĠinĠtheĠperformanceĠautomotiveĠcommunity.

ĠC antonĠRacingĠProductsĠhasĠbeenĠbuildingĠoilĠpansĠandĠengineĠrelatedĠproductsĠforĠracingĠandĠhighĠperformanceĠapplicationsĠsinceĠ1981.ĠWeĠbeganĠinĠaĠsmallĠConnecticutĠgarageĠbuildingĠspecialtyĠoilĠpansĠforĠlocalĠautoĠracers.ĠTheĠuniqueĠoilĠpansĠprovidedĠracersĠwithĠtheĠpowerĠandĠqualityĠtheyĠdemanded.ĠAsĠpopularityĠforĠtheĠspecialtyĠoilĠpansĠgrewĠsoĠdidĠourĠselectionĠofĠproducts.ĠTodayĠweĠofferĠaĠwideĠrangeĠofĠhighĠperformanceĠproductsĠforĠracingĠandĠtheĠstreet.ĠDuringĠourĠbusinessĠhoursĠeveryĠphoneĠcallĠisĠdirectedĠstraightĠtoĠourĠhardĠworkingĠsalesĠteam.ĠTheyĠareĠhappyĠtoĠuseĠtheirĠexperienceĠandĠknowledgeĠinĠtheĠautomotiveĠmarketĠtoĠprovideĠcustomerĠservice,ĠproductĠadvice,ĠandĠtechnicalĠsupportĠtoĠyouĠandĠyourĠcustomer.ĠOurĠproductionĠprocessĠfocusesĠonĠaccuracyĠandĠreliability.ĠEveryĠproductĠweĠmakeĠisĠbuiltĠwithĠtheĠsameĠproductionĠandĠqualityĠassuranceĠmethodsĠthatĠweĠuseĠwhenĠbuildingĠpartsĠforĠFord,ĠRoush,ĠandĠMopar.ĠAllĠproductsĠareĠtigĠwelded,ĠratherĠthenĠmigĠwelded.ĠTheĠtigĠweldingĠprocessĠtakesĠmoreĠtimeĠandĠskillĠbutĠensuresĠmoreĠevenĠheatĠandĠpenetrationĠthroughĠoutĠtheĠweldingĠprocess.ĠThisĠresultĠisĠbetterĠqualityĠweldsĠwithĠlessĠpossibilityĠforĠleaksĠandĠcracks.ĠEveryĠoilĠpan,ĠvalveĠcover,ĠandĠtankĠthatĠweĠproduceĠunderĠgoesĠseveralĠleakĠtests.ĠOurĠoilĠpansĠandĠvalveĠcoversĠareĠfittedĠonĠblocksĠorĠheadsĠseveralĠtimesĠthroughĠoutĠtheĠproductionĠprocessĠtoĠensureĠtheyĠeasilyĠinstallĠonĠtheirĠapplication.ĠWeĠhaveĠbeenĠactivelyĠinvolvedĠinĠracingĠforĠdecades.ĠOverĠtheĠyearsĠweĠhaveĠbuiltĠandĠranĠseveralĠcarsĠandĠhaveĠanĠappreciationĠforĠtheĠeffortĠandĠdedicationĠitĠtakesĠcompete.ĠWeĠactivelyĠparticipateĠwithĠclubs,Ġschools,ĠandĠotherĠorganizationsĠinĠtheĠperformanceĠautomotiveĠcommunity.

IfĠyouĠchooseĠtheĠâĢľMatteĠPaperĠPrint,ĠNoĠFrameâĢĿĠoption,ĠyouĠwillĠreceiveĠanĠunframedĠprintĠofĠyourĠchosenĠdesign.ĠTheĠpaperĠweĠuseĠtoĠprintĠonĠisĠ250ĠGSMĠmuseum-quality,Ġthick,Ġdurable,ĠmatteĠpaperĠ(non-reflectiveĠ&Ġnon-glossy).ĠTheĠinksĠweĠuseĠareĠhigh-qualityĠandĠUVĠprotected,ĠtheyĠwillĠlastĠaĠlifetime.ĠThisĠoptionĠisĠcommonlyĠchosenĠbyĠthoseĠwhoĠwishĠtoĠframeĠtheĠdesignĠthemselves.Packaging:âĢľMatteĠPaperĠPrint,ĠNoĠFrameâĢĿĠordersĠareĠshippedĠflatĠbetweenĠultra-toughĠcardboardĠsheets.ĠB1ĠandĠA0ĠsizesĠareĠshippedĠcarefullyĠrolledĠinĠlargeĠtubes.ĠStretchedĠ&ĠMountedĠCanvas:IfĠyouĠchooseĠtheĠâĢľStretchedĠ&ĠMountedĠCanvasâĢĿĠoption,ĠyourĠorderĠwillĠbeĠprintedĠofĠhigh-qualityĠcanvasĠmaterial,Ġgallery-wrapped,ĠstretchedĠandĠmountedĠaroundĠaĠwoodenĠframe.WeĠuseĠpremium-grade,Ġ360gsmĠcanvasĠmaterial.Gallery-wrappedĠonĠaĠ3cmĠdeepĠwoodenĠframe.StretchedĠCanvasĠordersĠarriveĠreadyĠtoĠhang.OptionalĠFramedĠCanvas:ThereĠisĠanĠoptionĠtoĠhaveĠyourĠâĢľStretchedĠ&ĠMountedĠCanvasâĢĿĠframed.ĠThisĠisĠcommonlyĠcalledĠaĠâĢľFloatingĠCanvasâĢĿĠstyle.ĠThereĠisĠanĠexampleĠphotographĠofĠwhatĠthisĠlooksĠlikeĠinĠtheĠproductĠimageĠsectionĠaboveĠ(theĠ7thĠproductĠimage,ĠshowingĠtheĠDarkĠOakĠframeĠaroundĠtheĠStretchedĠCanvas).ĠYouĠcanĠchooseĠbetweenĠaĠâĢľWhiteâĢĿ,ĠâĢľBlackâĢĿĠorĠâĢľDarkĠOakâĢĿĠcolourĠframe.ĠâĢľLightĠOakâĢĿĠisĠnotĠavailableĠasĠaĠcolourĠoptionĠforĠâĢľStretchedĠ&ĠMountedĠCanvasâĢĿ.PleaseĠnote:ĠâĢľStretchedĠ&ĠMountedĠCanvasâĢĿĠordersĠtakeĠ2-3ĠbusinessĠdaysĠlongerĠthanĠourĠnormalĠfulfilmentĠtimeframesĠandĠareĠsometimesĠsentĠwithĠcouriersĠotherĠthanĠAustraliaĠPost.
